10:["$","p","p-1",{"children":"The auction house is where players can list their items and people can bid on it. As a semi-automated system, there are some mishaps (items being sold for too little, too high) for valuation of items. There are two types of auctions: regular auction and Buy-it-now (BIN) auctions. Regular auctions are what they imply: players bidding each other out until the final bid value. BIN auctions are where an item can be bought instantly if the listed price is paid. While BIN auctions were introduced later, they are now much more popular. This is probably since the risk of an item being sold with a low bid is reduced. BIN auctions can expire but they can't be sold for lower than the listed price, which is reassuring to most people."}]

However, only commodities (ex: wheat, mutton, ...) can only be traded, which does not include skins and most other items. Since it's so inconvenient, and I'm not experienced enough to talk about it, I'll probably sav eit for a later post."}]
